         <h1 class="article_title" itemprop="headline name">

          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Baseball memorabilia has come in many forms through the years, and there has always been a market out there willing to meet the various offerings of baseball cards, programs, shirts, autographed balls, autographed bats and a wide assortment of other items.
           </p>
           <p>
            Today's market for baseball memorabilia and novelties has grown exponentially, and in spite of a recent economy that crippled the country, the industry still thrives. Now, there are literally thousands of different items connected to baseball teams and licensed by MLB that can be purchased.
           </p>
           <p>
            While the memorabilia industry may have been dominated by more serious baseball fans in years past, technology and innovative marketing have recently made baseball memorabilia much more popular among casual baseball fans as well.
           </p>
           <p>
            Today, Bleacher Report will take a look at the hot items that baseball fans seem to be drawn to these days. The list was culled by performing exhaustive research (well, maybe not exhaustive, but it sure did exhaust me), and compiling lists from eBay as to what the current trends are in the memorabilia market.
           </p>
           <p>
            Here, then, is our list of the Top 50 best baseball novelties that you can purchase right now.
           </p>
           <p>
            <em>
             Doug Mead is a featured columnist with Bleacher Report. His work has been featured on the Seattle Post-Intelligencer, SF Gate, CBS Sports, the Los Angeles Times and the Houston Chronicle. Follow Doug on Twitter,
             <a href="http://twitter.com/Sports_A_Holic">
              @Sports_A_Holic
             </a>
             .
            </em>
           </p>
          </div>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             50. Philadelphia Phillies Licensed Quilt Purse/Handbag: $21.89
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:400px">
            <img alt="50. Philadelphia Phillies Licensed Quilt Purse/Handbag: $21.89" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/041/140/PhiladelphiaPhilliesQuiltedPurse-Handbag_crop_400x400.jpg?1308791383" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="400"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Ladies, its not a Prada, or a Nine West, or even a Gucci. But it is licensed. MLB-licensed, that is.
           </p>
           <p>
            This catchy little purse comes with a magnetic snap closure, interior pocket and even an adjustable strap. Its even officially licensed by MLB, so ladies, you can look stylish walking through the streets of Philly while proudly displaying your love of Phillies baseball.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

             49. New York Yankees Desk Lamp: $24.99
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="49. New York Yankees Desk Lamp: $24.99" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/041/143/MLBNYYankeesDeskLamp_crop_630x420.jpg?1308791481" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Is there really anything quite like illuminating your desk area and proudly showing your Yankee colors? With this niftly little New York Yankees desk lamp, that can happen in a flash of light, so to speak.
           </p>
           <p>
            This item, also officially licensed by MLB, is available in the colors of other teams as well.
           </p>

             45. MLB Team Logo BBQ Gas Grill Cover: $18.50
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="45. MLB Team Logo BBQ Gas Grill Cover: $18.50" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/041/170/NewYorkYankeesGasGrillCover_crop_630x420.jpg?1308791914" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Even your outdoor cooking apparatus can be accessorized with your favorite MLB team colors. Your barbeque gas grill can now be covered against the elements sporting your favorite MLB team logo.
           </p>
           <p>
            Maybe you can get matching MLB logo barbeque tongs, or maybe if youre really lucky, you can find some charcoal briquettes emblazoned with your favorite team logo as well. How cool would that be, to see your team going up in flames every time you light the grill?
           </p>

            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>

           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="43. MLB Baltimore Orioles 30 X 60 Beach Towel" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/041/184/MLBBaltimoreOrioles30x60BeachTowel_crop_630x420.jpg?1308792189" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

             28. Boston Red Sox Solid Pewter Key Ring
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:315px">
            <img alt="28. Boston Red Sox Solid Pewter Key Ring" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/041/591/MLBBostonRedSoxPewterKeyRing_crop_315x420.jpg?1308802839" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="315"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            With this particular MLB novelty item, you not only get the Boston Red Sox logo; you also get a likeness of the Boston skyline, and the key ring is made out of solid pewter.
           </p>
           <p>
            For those of you not familiar with history, making things out of pewter was the chosen profession of Revolutionary War figure Paul Revere.
           </p>
           <p>
            Look at that. Everything about Boston is covered in one single key ring.
           </p>
          </div>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             7. One Dozen Rawlings Official MLB Baseballs: $159.00
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="7. One Dozen Rawlings Official MLB Baseballs: $159.00" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/042/503/RawlingsOfficialBaseballs1Dozen_crop_630x420.jpg?1308844577" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            So, for the price of a hot dog and a beer (well, maybe two hot dogs and a beer), you can purchase your own set of the baseballs the pros use.
           </p>
           <p>
            Alternatively, you could go to the ballpark and wait for the players and ball boys to throw literally dozens of the same balls into the bleachers.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            </h2>
           </div>

            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">

Mark McGwire Action Figure: $5.99" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/042/565/MarkMcGwireActionFigure_crop_630x420.jpg?1308845724" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

             1. MLB Titanium Necklace: $10.00
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:500px">
            <img alt="1. MLB Titanium Necklace: $10.00" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/042/595/MLBTitaniumNecklace_crop_500x375.jpg?1308845871" height="375" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="500"/>

          </div>

    (function(){
        // If we've already installed the SDK, we're done
        if (document.getElementById('facebook-jssdk')) {return;}

        // Get the first script element, which we'll use to find the parent node
